local function _CX_b64d(s)
  local b="ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/"
  s=s:gsub("[^"..b.."=]","")
  local out=""
  s:gsub(".?.?.?.",function(c)
    if c=="" then return end
    local n=0
    c:gsub(".",function(ch)
      if ch=="=" then n=n*64
      else n=n*64+(b:find(ch)-1) end
    end)
    out=out..string.char(math.floor(n/65536)%256,math.floor(n/256)%256,n%256)
  end)
  return out:gsub("\0+$","")
end
